./src/stories/components/AppHeader.stories.tsx:
import type { Meta, StoryObj } from '@storybook/react-vite';
import { Search, Bell, Moon, Sun, PanelLeft } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';

const meta: Meta = {
  title: 'Design System / Componentes / AppHeader',
  tags: ['autodocs'],
  parameters: {
    layout: 'fullscreen',
    docs: {
      description: {
        component: `
## AppHeader — Barra Superior

Barra de navegação superior da aplicação Horizon.

### Anatomia
- **Esquerda**: SidebarTrigger + Breadcrumbs
- **Direita**: Busca · Notificações · Toggle Tema · Avatar

### Regra de hover para ícones
Todo botão de ícone no header usa o padrão:

\`\`\`tsx
className="text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground"
\`\`\`

Isso garante que o ícone fique **branco** sobre o fundo **navy escuro** do \`--accent\`
tanto em **light mode** quanto em **dark mode**.

| Token | Light Mode | Dark Mode |
|-------|-----------|-----------|
| \`--accent\` | \`210 50% 24%\` (navy) | \`210 50% 24%\` (navy) |
| \`--accent-foreground\` | \`0 0% 100%\` (branco) | \`38 30% 93%\` (creme) |

> **Nunca usar** \`hover:text-foreground\` em ícones sobre fundo accent — o foreground
> em light mode é navy escuro, invisível sobre fundo navy.
        `,
      },
    },
  },
};
export default meta;
type Story = StoryObj;

const HeaderPreview = ({ theme }: { theme: 'light' | 'dark' }) => (
  <header className="h-14 border-b border-border flex items-center justify-between px-4 bg-background-secondary">
    {/* Esquerda */}
    <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
      <Button
        variant="ghost"
        size="icon"
        aria-label="Alternar sidebar"
        className="text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground"
      >
        <PanelLeft className="h-4 w-4" />
      </Button>
      <nav aria-label="Breadcrumb">
        <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Dashboard</span>
      </nav>
    </div>

    {/* Direita */}
    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
      <Button
        variant="ghost"
        size="icon"
        aria-label="Buscar"
        className="text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground"
      >
        <Search className="h-4 w-4" />
      </Button>
      <Button
        variant="ghost"
        size="icon"
        aria-label="Notificações"
        className="text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground"
      >
        <Bell className="h-4 w-4" />
      </Button>
      <Button
        variant="ghost"
        size="icon"
        aria-label="Alternar tema"
        className="text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground"
      >
        {theme === 'dark' ? <Sun className="h-4 w-4" /> : <Moon className="h-4 w-4" />}
      </Button>
      <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-primary flex items-center justify-center text-primary-foreground text-xs font-heading font-bold ml-2">
        H
      </div>
    </div>
  </header>
);

export const LightMode: Story = {
  name: 'Light Mode',
  render: (_, context) => (
    <HeaderPreview theme={(context.globals.theme as 'light' | 'dark') ?? 'light'} />
  ),
};

  name: 'Dark Mode',
  globals: { theme: 'dark' },
  render: (_, context) => (
    <HeaderPreview theme={(context.globals.theme as 'light' | 'dark') ?? 'dark'} />
  ),
};

  // Navigation & layout
  ChevronRight, ChevronDown, ChevronLeft, ChevronUp,

/* ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 * Utilitários de download
 *
 * • SVG  — serializa o <svg> que já está renderizado no DOM, força um
 *          viewBox/size de 24x24 e estiliza com stroke="currentColor"
 *          (que resolve para preto quando o SVG é aberto isoladamente).
 *          Fundo SEMPRE transparente (não há <rect> de background).
 *
 * • PNG  — converte o mesmo SVG em data URL, carrega numa <img>, desenha
 *          em um <canvas> de 512x512 e exporta via canvas.toBlob('image/png').
 *          Canvas tem fundo transparente por padrão (não preenchemos).
 * ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

function triggerDownload(url: string, filename: string) {
  const a = document.createElement("a");
  a.href = url;
  a.download = filename;
  document.body.appendChild(a);
  a.click();
  document.body.removeChild(a);
}

function buildExportableSvg(svgEl: SVGSVGElement, sizePx: number): string {
  const clone = svgEl.cloneNode(true) as SVGSVGElement;
  // Garante atributos essenciais para uso isolado
  clone.setAttribute("xmlns", "http://www.w3.org/2000/svg");
  clone.setAttribute("width", String(sizePx));
  clone.setAttribute("height", String(sizePx));
  // Lucide usa stroke="currentColor"; ao abrir o SVG isolado, currentColor
  // fica preto. Se quiser garantir, descomente a linha abaixo.
  // clone.setAttribute("color", "#000");
  if (!clone.getAttribute("viewBox")) {
    clone.setAttribute("viewBox", "0 0 24 24");
  }
  // Remove classes do React/Tailwind (cosmético — não afeta render isolado)
  clone.removeAttribute("class");
  return new XMLSerializer().serializeToString(clone);
}

function downloadIconAsSvg(svgEl: SVGSVGElement, name: string) {
  const svgString = buildExportableSvg(svgEl, 24);
  const xml = '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>\n' + svgString;
  const blob = new Blob([xml], { type: "image/svg+xml;charset=utf-8" });
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  triggerDownload(url, `${name}.svg`);
  // Pequeno delay para garantir que o navegador iniciou o download antes do revoke
  window.setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(url), 1000);
}

function downloadIconAsPng(svgEl: SVGSVGElement, name: string, sizePx = 512) {
  const svgString = buildExportableSvg(svgEl, sizePx);
  const svgBlob = new Blob([svgString], { type: "image/svg+xml;charset=utf-8" });
  const svgUrl = URL.createObjectURL(svgBlob);

  const img = new Image();
  img.crossOrigin = "anonymous";
  img.onload = () => {
    const canvas = document.createElement("canvas");
    canvas.width = sizePx;
    canvas.height = sizePx;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");
    if (!ctx) {
      URL.revokeObjectURL(svgUrl);
      return;
    }
    // NÃO preenchemos o canvas → fundo permanece transparente
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, sizePx, sizePx);
    ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, sizePx, sizePx);
    URL.revokeObjectURL(svgUrl);

    canvas.toBlob((blob) => {
      if (!blob) return;
      const pngUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
      triggerDownload(pngUrl, `${name}.png`);
      window.setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(pngUrl), 1000);
    }, "image/png");
  };
  img.onerror = () => URL.revokeObjectURL(svgUrl);
  img.src = svgUrl;
}

/* ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 * Card individual de ícone
 * ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

interface IconCardProps {
  name: string;
  Icon: React.ElementType;
  query: string;
  isCopied: boolean;
  onCopy: (name: string) => void;
}

function IconCard({ name, Icon, query, isCopied, onCopy }: IconCardProps) {
  const ref = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  const getSvgEl = (): SVGSVGElement | null => {
    return (ref.current?.querySelector("svg") as SVGSVGElement | null) ?? null;
  };

  const handleDownloadSvg = (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    const svg = getSvgEl();
    if (svg) downloadIconAsSvg(svg, name);
  };

  const handleDownloadPng = (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    const svg = getSvgEl();
    if (svg) downloadIconAsPng(svg, name);
  };

  return (
    <div
      ref={ref}
      className={`relative group/card rounded-lg border bg-card transition-colors ${
        isCopied
          ? "border-primary bg-primary/10"
          : "border-border hover:bg-accent/30"
      }`}
    >
      {/* Action buttons — visíveis no hover */}
      <div
        className="absolute top-1 right-1 z-10 flex gap-0.5 opacity-0 group-hover/card:opacity-100 focus-within:opacity-100 transition-opacity"
        onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
      >
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={handleDownloadSvg}
          title={`Baixar ${name}.svg (fundo transparente)`}
          aria-label={`Baixar ${name} como SVG transparente`}
          className="px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[9px] font-mono font-semibold rounded bg-background/90 backdrop-blur-sm border border-border text-muted-foreground hover:bg-primary hover:text-primary-foreground hover:border-primary transition-colors"
        >
          SVG
        </button>
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={handleDownloadPng}
          title={`Baixar ${name}.png 512px (fundo transparente)`}
          aria-label={`Baixar ${name} como PNG transparente`}
          className="px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[9px] font-mono font-semibold rounded bg-background/90 backdrop-blur-sm border border-border text-muted-foreground hover:bg-primary hover:text-primary-foreground hover:border-primary transition-colors"
        >
          PNG
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Body — clique copia o nome */}
      <button
        type="button"
        onClick={() => onCopy(name)}
        title={isCopied ? "Copiado!" : `Clique para copiar "${name}"`}
        className="w-full flex flex-col items-center gap-2 p-3 cursor-pointer text-left bg-transparent rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-ring"
      >
        <Icon
          className={`h-5 w-5 ${
            isCopied ? "text-primary" : "text-foreground"
          }`}
        />
        <span className="text-[9px] text-muted-foreground font-mono text-center leading-tight break-all">
          {isCopied ? (
            <span className="text-primary font-semibold">Copiado!</span>
          ) : (
            <HighlightedName name={name} query={query} />
          )}
        </span>
      </button>
    </div>
  );
}

/**
 * Destaca o trecho do nome que casou com a busca, sem usar `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`.
 */
function HighlightedName({ name, query }: { name: string; query: string }) {
  if (!query) return <>{name}</>;
  const idx = name.toLowerCase().indexOf(query.toLowerCase());
  if (idx === -1) return <>{name}</>;
  return (
    <>
      {name.slice(0, idx)}
      <mark className="bg-primary/30 text-primary rounded-sm px-0.5">
        {name.slice(idx, idx + query.length)}
      </mark>
      {name.slice(idx + query.length)}
    </>
  );
}

function IconGrid() {
  const [query, setQuery] = useState("");
  const [copied, setCopied] = useState<string | null>(null);

  /** Filtra grupos e seus ícones — esconde grupos sem matches. */
  const filteredGroups = useMemo(() => {
    const q = query.trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!q) return iconGroups;
    return iconGroups
      .map((g) => ({
        ...g,
        icons: g.icons.filter((i) => i.name.toLowerCase().includes(q)),
      }))
      .filter((g) => g.icons.length > 0);
  }, [query]);

  const totalIcons = useMemo(
    () => iconGroups.reduce((sum, g) => sum + g.icons.length, 0),
    [],
  );
  const matchedCount = useMemo(
    () => filteredGroups.reduce((sum, g) => sum + g.icons.length, 0),
    [filteredGroups],
  );

  const copyName = async (name: string) => {
    try {
      await navigator.clipboard.writeText(name);
      setCopied(name);
      window.setTimeout(() => setCopied((c) => (c === name ? null : c)), 1200);
    } catch {
      /* clipboard pode estar bloqueado */
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="p-2">
      {/* ─── Search bar (sticky no topo) ─────────────────────────────────── */}
      <div className="sticky top-0 z-10 -mx-2 px-2 py-3 mb-6 bg-background/95 backdrop-blur supports-[backdrop-filter]:bg-background/80 border-b border-border">
        <div className="relative">
          <Search className="pointer-events-none absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 h-4 w-4 text-muted-foreground" />
          <input
            type="search"
            value={query}
            onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="Buscar ícone por nome (ex.: chevron, user, file)…"
            aria-label="Buscar ícone"
            autoFocus
            className="w-full h-10 pl-9 pr-24 rounded-md border border-input bg-background text-sm text-foreground placeholder:text-muted-foreground focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 focus:ring-offset-background"
          />
          {query && (
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={() => setQuery("")}
              aria-label="Limpar busca"
              className="absolute right-2 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center h-6 w-6 rounded hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground"
            >
              <X className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
            </button>
          )}
        </div>

        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mt-2 px-1">
          <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground">
            {query ? (
              <>
                <span className="text-foreground font-semibold">{matchedCount}</span>{" "}
                de {totalIcons} ícones · clique para copiar nome · passe o mouse
                e clique <span className="font-mono text-foreground">SVG</span>/
                <span className="font-mono text-foreground">PNG</span> para baixar
              </>
            ) : (
              <>
                <span className="text-foreground font-semibold">{totalIcons}</span>{" "}
                ícones · clique para copiar nome · passe o mouse e clique{" "}
                <span className="font-mono text-foreground">SVG</span>/
                <span className="font-mono text-foreground">PNG</span> para baixar
                (fundo transparente)
              </>
            )}
          </p>
          {query && matchedCount === 0 && (
            <p className="text-[11px] text-warning">Nenhum ícone encontrado</p>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* ─── Grids por grupo ─────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
      {filteredGroups.length === 0 ? (
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center py-16 px-4 text-center">
          <Search className="h-10 w-10 text-muted-foreground/50 mb-3" />
          <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">
            Nenhum ícone corresponde a “{query}”
          </p>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
            Verifique a grafia (PascalCase) ou tente um termo mais curto.
          </p>
          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={() => setQuery("")}
            className="mt-4 text-xs font-medium text-primary hover:underline"
          >
            Limpar busca
          </button>
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="space-y-10">
          {filteredGroups.map((group) => (
            <div key={group.label}>
              <h3 className="text-xs font-heading font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-4">
                {group.label}{" "}
                <span className="text-muted-foreground/60 normal-case font-normal">
                  ({group.icons.length})
                </span>
              </h3>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-4 sm:grid-cols-6 md:grid-cols-8 lg:grid-cols-10 gap-2">
                {group.icons.map(({ name, icon: Icon }) => (
                  <IconCard
                    key={name}
                    name={name}
                    Icon={Icon}
                    query={query}
                    isCopied={copied === name}
                    onCopy={copyName}
                  />
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

  name: "Todos os Ícones",
  render: () => <IconGrid />,
};

import type { Meta, StoryObj } from "@storybook/react-vite";
import { ThemeProvider } from "@/contexts/ThemeContext";
import CadastroAtivos from "@/pages/cadastro/CadastroAtivos";
import CadastroBankerAssessor from "@/pages/cadastro/CadastroBankerAssessor";

  <ThemeProvider>
    <div className="p-6 bg-background min-h-screen">
      <Story />
    </div>
  </ThemeProvider>
);

    },
  },
  tags: ["autodocs"],

  const [checked, setChecked] = useState(false);
  return (
    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
      <Checkbox
        id="aceito"
        checked={checked}
        onCheckedChange={(v) => setChecked(!!v)}
      />
      <Label htmlFor="aceito" className="cursor-pointer select-none">
        Aceito os termos de uso
      </Label>
    </div>
  );

Lista com selecionar todos story ok 
const ListaSelecionavel = () => {
  const items = ["BOL-413", "BOL-414", "BOL-415", "BOL-416"];
  const [sel, setSel] = useState<string[]>([]);
  const allChecked = sel.length === items.length;
  const indeterminate = sel.length > 0 && !allChecked;
  const checkedValue: boolean | "indeterminate" = allChecked
    ? true
    : indeterminate
      ? "indeterminate"
      : false;

  return (
    <div className="w-64 space-y-2">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 border-b border-border pb-2">
        <Checkbox
          id="all"
          checked={checkedValue}
          onCheckedChange={(v) => {
            if (v === true) setSel(items);
            else setSel([]);
          }}
        />
        <Label htmlFor="all" className="cursor-pointer text-sm font-heading">
          Selecionar todas ({sel.length}/{items.length})
        </Label>
      </div>
      {items.map((it) => (
        <div key={it} className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Checkbox
            id={it}
            checked={sel.includes(it)}
            onCheckedChange={(v) =>
              setSel((prev) => (v ? [...prev, it] : prev.filter((x) => x !== it)))
            }
          />
          <Label htmlFor={it} className="cursor-pointer font-mono text-sm">
            {it}
          </Label>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
};

function isLight(hex: string) {
  const r = parseInt(hex.slice(1, 3), 16);
  const g = parseInt(hex.slice(3, 5), 16);
  const b = parseInt(hex.slice(5, 7), 16);
  return (r * 299 + g * 587 + b * 114) / 1000 > 128;
}

function Swatch({ shade, hex, label }: { shade: string; hex: string; label?: string }) {
  const textColor = isLight(hex) ? '#111827' : '#F9FAFB';
  return (
    <div
      style={{ backgroundColor: hex, color: textColor }}
      className="flex flex-col justify-end p-3 rounded-lg min-h-[80px] relative"
      title={hex}
    >
      {label && (
        <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider opacity-80 mb-0.5">
          {label}
        </span>
      )}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <span className="text-sm font-semibold">{shade}</span>
        <span className="text-xs font-mono opacity-70">{hex}</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function Palette({ name, swatches }: { name: string; swatches: { shade: string; hex: string; label?: string }[] }) {
  return (
    <div className="mb-10">
      <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold uppercase tracking-widest text-muted-foreground mb-3">{name}</h3>
      <div className="grid grid-cols-11 gap-2">
        {swatches.map((s) => (
          <Swatch key={s.shade} {...s} />
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

const TABLE_TOKENS = [
  {
    name: 'Row Group Header',
    var: '--row-group-header',
    cssVar: 'hsl(var(--row-group-header))',
    desc:
      'Fundo do header de agrupamento em tabelas hierárquicas (ex.: linha-pai do cliente em ClientesTable, ou da solicitação em BoletadorTable). Diferenciado do `--secondary` para garantir contraste com o sub-header de colunas em ambos light/dark.',
    used: 'ClientesTable · BoletadorTable',
  },
  {
    name: 'Card (sub-header)',
    var: '--card',
    cssVar: 'hsl(var(--card))',
    desc:
      'Fundo padrão de cards. Em tabelas hierárquicas, é também o fundo do cabeçalho de colunas e das linhas-filhas — garante contraste com `--row-group-header`.',
    used: 'Card · Tabela sub-header · Linhas filhas',
  },
  {
    name: 'Muted (hover)',
    var: '--muted',
    cssVar: 'hsl(var(--muted))',
    desc: 'Fundo de hover em linhas e elementos desabilitados.',
    used: 'Hover de linha · Skeletons',
  },
  {
    name: 'Border',
    var: '--border',
    cssVar: 'hsl(var(--border))',
    desc: 'Bordas padrão entre linhas e em volta de cards.',
    used: 'Bordas de tabela',
  },
];

function TableTokenSwatch({
  name,
  cssVar,
  varName,
  desc,
  used,
}: {
  name: string;
  cssVar: string;
  varName: string;
  desc: string;
  used: string;
}) {
  return (
    <div className="flex items-start gap-4 p-4 rounded-xl border bg-card">
      <div
        className="w-14 h-14 rounded-lg flex-shrink-0 border border-border"
        style={{ backgroundColor: cssVar }}
      />
      <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
        <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-foreground">{name}</p>
        <p className="text-xs font-mono text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">{varName}</p>
        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">{desc}</p>
        <p className="text-[11px] text-primary mt-1">
          <span className="opacity-70">Usado em:</span> {used}
        </p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function SemanticSwatch({ name, cssVar, desc }: { name: string; cssVar: string; desc: string }) {
  return (
    <div className="flex items-start gap-4 p-4 rounded-xl border bg-card">
      <div
        className="w-14 h-14 rounded-lg flex-shrink-0 border border-black/10"
        style={{ backgroundColor: `var(${cssVar})` }}
      />
      <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
        <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-foreground">{name}</p>
        <p className="text-xs font-mono text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">{cssVar}</p>
        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">{desc}</p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

          { label: 'Neutro',  text: 'text-gray-600',   bg: 'bg-gray-100',   border: 'border-gray-200',   desc: 'Rascunho · Arquivado · Inativo' },
        ].map(({ label, text, bg, border, desc }) => (
          <div key={label} className={`flex items-center gap-4 px-4 py-3 rounded-xl border ${bg} ${border}`}>
            <span className={`text-sm font-semibold w-20 ${text}`}>{label}</span>
            <span className={`text-xs px-2.5 py-0.5 rounded-full border font-medium ${bg} ${border} ${text}`}>{label}</span>
            <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{desc}</span>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
);

const ComCheckbox = () => {
  const [cols, setCols] = useState({ ativo: true, tipo: true, qtd: true, status: true });
  return (
    <DropdownMenu>
      <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
        <Button variant="outline" size="sm">
          Colunas visíveis
        </Button>
      </DropdownMenuTrigger>
      <DropdownMenuContent align="start" className="w-48">
        <DropdownMenuLabel>Mostrar colunas</DropdownMenuLabel>
        <DropdownMenuSeparator />
        {Object.entries(cols).map(([key, value]) => (
          <DropdownMenuCheckboxItem
            key={key}
            checked={value}
            onCheckedChange={(checked) =>
              setCols((p) => ({ ...p, [key]: !!checked }))
            }
          >
            {key.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + key.slice(1)}
          </DropdownMenuCheckboxItem>
        ))}
      </DropdownMenuContent>
    </DropdownMenu>
  );
};

Single — Tipo de Ativo story ok 
const SingleSelect = () => {
  const [value, setValue] = useState('');
  const [options, setOptions] = useState([
    'Ação', 'Fundo', 'FII', 'Renda Fixa', 'Tesouro Direto',
    'ETF', 'BDR', 'Cripto',
  ]);
  return (
    <div className="w-80 space-y-2">
      <Label className="font-heading text-sm">
        Tipo <span className="text-destructive">*</span>
      </Label>
      <EditableSelect
        options={options}
        value={value}
        onValueChange={setValue}
        onCreateOption={(n) => setOptions((p) => [...p, n])}
        onDeleteOption={(n) => setOptions((p) => p.filter((x) => x !== n))}
        placeholder="Selecione o tipo"
        createLabel="Criar novo tipo"
        itemLabel="tipo"
      />
      <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
        Selecionado: <code className="text-primary">{value || '—'}</code>
      </p>
    </div>
  );
};

        options={options}
        values={values}
        onChange={setValues}
        onCreateOption={(n) => setOptions((p) => [...p, n])}
        onDeleteOption={(n) => setOptions((p) => p.filter((x) => x !== n))}
        placeholder="Selecione um ou mais mercados"
        createLabel="Criar novo mercado"
        itemLabel="mercado"
      />
      <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
        Selecionados:{" "}
        <code className="text-primary">
          {values.length > 0 ? values.join(', ') : '—'}
        </code>

    </div>
  );

const CombinedExample = () => {
  const [tipo, setTipo] = useState('');
  const [moeda, setMoeda] = useState('');
  const [mercados, setMercados] = useState<string[]>([]);

  const [tipos, setTipos] = useState(['Ação', 'FII', 'BDR', 'ETF']);
  const [moedas, setMoedas] = useState(['BRL', 'USD', 'EUR']);
  const [mercadosOpts, setMercadosOpts] = useState([
    'B3', 'Anbima', 'BM&F', 'NYSE',
  ]);

  return (
    <div className="max-w-3xl mx-auto p-6 space-y-6 bg-card border border-border rounded-lg">
      <h2 className="font-heading text-lg font-semibold text-foreground">
        Exemplo combinado — Novo Ativo
      </h2>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
        <div className="space-y-1.5">
          <Label className="font-heading text-sm">
            Tipo <span className="text-destructive">*</span>
          </Label>
          <EditableSelect
            options={tipos}
            value={tipo}
            onValueChange={setTipo}
            onCreateOption={(n) => setTipos((p) => [...p, n])}
            onDeleteOption={(n) => setTipos((p) => p.filter((x) => x !== n))}
            placeholder="Selecione o tipo"
            createLabel="Criar novo tipo"
            itemLabel="tipo"
          />
        </div>
        <div className="space-y-1.5">
          <Label className="font-heading text-sm">
            Moeda <span className="text-destructive">*</span>
          </Label>
          <EditableSelect
            options={moedas}
            value={moeda}
            onValueChange={setMoeda}
            onCreateOption={(n) => setMoedas((p) => [...p, n])}
            onDeleteOption={(n) => setMoedas((p) => p.filter((x) => x !== n))}
            placeholder="Selecione a moeda"
            createLabel="Criar nova moeda"
            itemLabel="moeda"
            createCase="upper"
          />
        </div>
        <div className="space-y-1.5">
          <Label className="font-heading text-sm">Mercados</Label>
          <EditableMultiSelect
            options={mercadosOpts}
            values={mercados}
            onChange={setMercados}
            onCreateOption={(n) => setMercadosOpts((p) => [...p, n])}
            onDeleteOption={(n) =>
              setMercadosOpts((p) => p.filter((x) => x !== n))
            }
            placeholder="Selecione um ou mais mercados"
            createLabel="Criar novo mercado"
            itemLabel="mercado"
          />
        </div>
      </div>

      <pre className="text-xs bg-muted/40 p-3 rounded border border-border">
{JSON.stringify({ tipo, moeda, mercados }, null, 2)}
      </pre>
    </div>
  );
};

import type { Meta, StoryObj } from '@storybook/react-vite';
import { useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import { Copy, Check, Mail } from 'lucide-react';
import {
  BOLETA_UPDATE_EMAIL_HTML,
  SAMPLE_BOLETA_VARS,
  renderBoletaUpdateEmail,
  type BoletaUpdateEmailVars,
} from '@/components/email-templates/BoletaUpdateEmail';

/* ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 * "Email Template" não é um componente React — é um template HTML inline,
 * compatível com Outlook / Gmail / Apple Mail, com placeholders Mustache.
 *
 * O Storybook renderiza o HTML dentro de um <iframe srcDoc=...> para
 * isolá-lo do CSS global e simular fielmente o ambiente de cliente de e-mail.
 * Cada variável (`{{boletaId}}`, `{{novoStatus}}`, etc.) é exposta como
 * control para edição em tempo real.
 * ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

interface EmailPreviewProps extends BoletaUpdateEmailVars {
  /** Altura do iframe de preview em pixels. */
  previewHeight?: number;
}

function EmailPreview({ previewHeight = 900, ...vars }: EmailPreviewProps) {
  const html = useMemo(() => renderBoletaUpdateEmail(vars), [vars]);

  return (
    <div className="w-full bg-[#f2efe9] py-6">
      <iframe
        title="Preview do e-mail"
        srcDoc={html}
        style={{
          width: '100%',
          height: previewHeight,
          border: 'none',
          display: 'block',
          backgroundColor: '#f2efe9',
        }}
        sandbox=""
      />
    </div>
  );
}

/* ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 * Visualizador do HTML cru — útil para copiar/colar em ferramentas de
 * envio (SMTP, SES, SendGrid, Mailchimp, etc.).
 * ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
function RawHtmlViewer() {
  const [copied, setCopied] = useState(false);

  const onCopy = async () => {
    try {
      await navigator.clipboard.writeText(BOLETA_UPDATE_EMAIL_HTML);
      setCopied(true);
      setTimeout(() => setCopied(false), 2000);
    } catch {
      /* clipboard pode ser bloqueado em sandbox */
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="relative w-full bg-zinc-950 text-zinc-100 rounded-lg border border-zinc-800 overflow-hidden">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 border-b border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900/60">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-zinc-400">
          <Mail className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
          <span className="font-mono">BoletaUpdateEmail.ts → BOLETA_UPDATE_EMAIL_HTML</span>
        </div>
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={onCopy}
          className="inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2.5 py-1 rounded-md bg-zinc-800 hover:bg-zinc-700 text-zinc-200 text-xs font-medium transition-colors"
        >
          {copied ? <Check className="h-3.5 w-3.5" /> : <Copy className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />}
          {copied ? 'Copiado' : 'Copiar HTML'}
        </button>
      </div>
      <pre className="text-[11px] leading-relaxed p-4 overflow-auto max-h-[600px]">
        <code>{BOLETA_UPDATE_EMAIL_HTML}</code>
      </pre>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 * Documentação inline com lista de variáveis e exemplo de uso.
 * ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
function UsageGuide() {
  const rows: { name: keyof BoletaUpdateEmailVars; example: string; desc: string }[] = [
    { name: 'boletaId',      example: 'BOL-1234',         desc: 'Identificador da boleta' },
    { name: 'solicitacaoId', example: 'SOL-9999',         desc: 'Identificador da solicitação-pai' },
    { name: 'novoStatus',    example: 'Executado',        desc: 'Nome do estágio atual no workflow' },
    { name: 'clienteFinal',  example: 'Carlos Silva',     desc: 'Nome do cliente final' },
    { name: 'instituicao',   example: 'XP Investimentos', desc: 'Instituição financeira' },
    { name: 'ativo',         example: 'ITUB4',            desc: 'Ticker do ativo' },
    { name: 'tipo',          example: 'COMPRA',           desc: 'COMPRA ou VENDA' },
    { name: 'qtd',           example: '2.500',            desc: 'Quantidade formatada' },
    { name: 'vlrFinan',      example: 'R$ 250.000,00',    desc: 'Valor financeiro formatado' },
  ];

  return (
    <div className="prose prose-sm max-w-none p-6 bg-card text-card-foreground rounded-lg border border-border space-y-4">
      <h3 className="text-base font-semibold text-foreground">Como reutilizar</h3>
      <pre className="text-xs bg-muted/40 p-3 rounded border border-border overflow-x-auto">
{`import {
  renderBoletaUpdateEmail,
  type BoletaUpdateEmailVars,
} from '@/components/email-templates/BoletaUpdateEmail';

const html = renderBoletaUpdateEmail({
  boletaId: 'BOL-1234',
  solicitacaoId: 'SOL-9999',
  novoStatus: 'Executado',
  clienteFinal: 'Carlos Silva',
  instituicao: 'XP Investimentos',
  ativo: 'ITUB4',
  tipo: 'COMPRA',
  qtd: '2.500',
  vlrFinan: 'R$ 250.000,00',
});

// Enviar via SMTP / SES / SendGrid / Resend ...
await ses.sendEmail({
  Destination: { ToAddresses: ['cliente@famicapital.com.br'] },
  Message: {
    Subject: { Data: 'Atualização de boleta' },
    Body: { Html: { Data: html } },
  },
  Source: 'no-reply@famicapital.com.br',
});`}
      </pre>

      <h3 className="text-base font-semibold text-foreground pt-2">Variáveis disponíveis</h3>
      <table className="w-full text-xs border border-border rounded">
        <thead>
          <tr className="bg-muted/40 text-foreground">
            <th className="text-left p-2 border-b border-border font-semibold">Variável</th>
            <th className="text-left p-2 border-b border-border font-semibold">Exemplo</th>
            <th className="text-left p-2 border-b border-border font-semibold">Descrição</th>
          </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
          {rows.map((r) => (
            <tr key={r.name} className="border-b border-border last:border-b-0">
              <td className="p-2 font-mono text-primary">{`{{${r.name}}}`}</td>
              <td className="p-2 text-muted-foreground">{r.example}</td>
              <td className="p-2 text-muted-foreground">{r.desc}</td>
            </tr>
          ))}
        </tbody>
      </table>

      <h3 className="text-base font-semibold text-foreground pt-2">Paleta da marca usada no e-mail</h3>
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-3 gap-2">
        {[
          { name: 'Navy (header / CTA)', hex: '#263C59', fg: '#fff' },
          { name: 'Gold (acento)',        hex: '#C19C63', fg: '#000' },
          { name: 'Background',           hex: '#f2efe9', fg: '#000' },
          { name: 'Card BG',              hex: '#fafaf7', fg: '#000' },
          { name: 'Card Border',          hex: '#ece7db', fg: '#000' },
          { name: 'Text Strong',          hex: '#0b0b0c', fg: '#fff' },
        ].map((c) => (
          <div
            key={c.hex}
            className="rounded border border-border overflow-hidden text-[11px]"
          >
            <div
              className="h-10 flex items-center justify-center font-mono"
              style={{ backgroundColor: c.hex, color: c.fg }}
            >
              {c.hex}
            </div>
            <div className="px-2 py-1 bg-card text-muted-foreground">{c.name}</div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

const meta: Meta<typeof EmailPreview> = {
  title: 'Design System / Identidade / Email Template',
  component: EmailPreview,
  tags: ['autodocs'],
  parameters: {
    layout: 'fullscreen',
    docs: {
      description: {
        component: `
## Email Template — Atualização de Boleta

Template HTML de e-mail transacional para notificar mudanças de status no
workflow do **Boletador**. É um \`.ts\` puro (sem React) que exporta:

- \`BOLETA_UPDATE_EMAIL_HTML\` — string HTML cru com placeholders \`{{var}}\`
- \`renderBoletaUpdateEmail(vars)\` — função utilitária para substituição
- \`SAMPLE_BOLETA_VARS\` — valores de exemplo para testes
- \`BoletaUpdateEmailVars\` — tipo TypeScript das variáveis

### Por que HTML inline?

Clientes de e-mail (especialmente Outlook) não suportam \`<style>\` externo
nem CSS moderno. O template usa \`<table>\` para layout e CSS inline para
máxima compatibilidade.

### Por que iframe no preview?

O Storybook é renderizado com Tailwind, e o HTML do e-mail tem CSS próprio
que conflita. O \`<iframe srcDoc>\` isola o documento, simulando fielmente
como o e-mail será exibido em Gmail / Outlook.
        `,
      },
    },
  },
  argTypes: {
    boletaId:      { control: 'text' },
    solicitacaoId: { control: 'text' },
    novoStatus: {
      control: 'select',
      options: ['Nova Solicitação', 'Em Execução', 'Executado', 'Replicado', 'Cancelado'],
    },
    clienteFinal: { control: 'text' },
    instituicao: {
      control: 'select',
      options: ['XP Investimentos', 'BTG Pactual', 'Itaú BBA', 'Bradesco BBI', 'Santander', 'Genial'],
    },
    ativo:    { control: 'text' },
    tipo:     { control: 'radio', options: ['COMPRA', 'VENDA'] },
    qtd:      { control: 'text' },
    vlrFinan: { control: 'text' },
    previewHeight: { control: { type: 'range', min: 600, max: 1400, step: 50 } },
  },
};

const Interativa = () => {
  const [search, setSearch] = useState("");
  return (
    <div className="space-y-4 w-[480px]">
      <FilterBar searchValue={search} onSearchChange={setSearch} />
      <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
        Valor atual:{" "}
        <strong className="text-foreground">{search || "(vazio)"}</strong>
      </p>
    </div>
  );
};
Exemplo — contexto de página story ok 
const ExemploPaginaCompleta = () => {
  const [search, setSearch] = useState("");
  const ativos = [
    "PETR4 — Petrobras PN",
    "VALE3 — Vale ON",
    "ITUB4 — Itaú PN",
    "BBDC4 — Bradesco PN",
    "WEGE3 — Weg ON",
  ].filter((a) => a.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()));

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4 w-[560px]">
      <FilterBar searchValue={search} onSearchChange={setSearch} />
      <ul className="space-y-1">
        {ativos.length > 0 ? (
          ativos.map((a) => (
            <li
              key={a}
              className="text-sm px-3 py-2 rounded-md border border-border bg-card text-foreground"
            >
              {a}
            </li>
          ))
        ) : (
          <li className="text-sm text-muted-foreground px-3 py-2">
            Nenhum ativo encontrado.
          </li>
        )}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
};

const Password = function PasswordStory() {
  const [show, setShow] = useState(false);
  return (
    <div className="w-72">
      <Label htmlFor="password-input">Senha</Label>
      <div className="relative mt-1.5">
        <Input id="password-input" type={show ? 'text' : 'password'} placeholder="••••••••" className="pr-10" />
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={() => setShow((v) => !v)}
          className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-ring rounded"
          aria-label={show ? 'Ocultar senha' : 'Mostrar senha'}
        >
          {show ? <EyeOff className="h-4 w-4" /> : <Eye className="h-4 w-4" />}
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

import type { Meta, StoryObj } from '@storybook/react-vite';
import { useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { MemoryRouter } from 'react-router-dom';
import { HorizonLoadingLogo } from '@/components/HorizonLoadingLogo';

const meta: Meta = {
  title: 'Design System / Páginas / Loading',
  tags: ['autodocs'],
  parameters: {
    layout: 'fullscreen',
    docs: {
      description: {
        component: `
## LoadingPage — Tela de transição pós-login

Tela exibida entre o login e o dashboard. Fundo navy \`rgb(28,48,73)\` com logo animado centralizado.

### Fluxo
\`/login\` → **\`/loading\`** (2.4s de animação) → \`/\` (Dashboard)

### Sequência de animação (Figma \`node-id=75-1291\` — Horizon-anima-2)

| Fase | Duração | Descrição |
|---|---|---|
| **Slide-up** | 0–850ms | Ícone do logo sobe de fora do frame com spring |
| **Cascata H** | 850ms | Letra H aparece com fade + translateY |
| **Cascata O** | 950ms | Letra O |
| **Cascata R** | 1050ms | Letra R |
| **Cascata I** | 1150ms | Letra I |
| **Cascata Z** | 1250ms | Letra Z |
| **Cascata O** | 1350ms | Letra O |
| **Cascata N** | 1450ms | Letra N |
| **onComplete** | ~2400ms | Callback disparado → navega para \`/\` |

### Props do HorizonLoadingLogo

| Prop | Tipo | Padrão | Descrição |
|---|---|---|---|
| \`height\` | \`number\` | \`80\` | Altura em px (largura proporcional 152:41) |
| \`onComplete\` | \`() => void\` | — | Callback após ~2.4s quando animação termina |

### Uso na LoadingPage

\`\`\`tsx
import { HorizonLoadingLogo } from '@/components/HorizonLoadingLogo';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';

export default function LoadingPage() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  return (
    <div
      className="fixed inset-0 flex items-center justify-center"
      style={{ backgroundColor: 'rgb(28,48,73)' }}
    >
      <HorizonLoadingLogo
        height={96}
        onComplete={() => navigate('/', { replace: true })}
      />
    </div>
  );
}
\`\`\`
        `,
      },
    },
  },
};
export default meta;
type Story = StoryObj;

/* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   Story 1 — Tela completa com replay
   ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
export const Default: Story = {
  name: 'Tela de Loading — Animação completa',
  render: () => {
    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/rules-of-hooks
    const [key, setKey] = useState(0);
    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/rules-of-hooks
    const [finished, setFinished] = useState(false);

    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/rules-of-hooks
    const replay = useCallback(() => {
      setFinished(false);
      setKey((k) => k + 1);
    }, []);

    return (
      <MemoryRouter>
        <div
          className="fixed inset-0 flex items-center justify-center"
          style={{ backgroundColor: 'rgb(28,48,73)' }}
        >
          <HorizonLoadingLogo
            key={key}
            height={96}
            onComplete={() => setFinished(true)}
          />

          {/* Botão de replay — aparece após animação terminar */}
          {finished && (
            <button
              onClick={replay}
              style={{
                position: 'absolute',
                bottom: 40,
                left: '50%',
                transform: 'translateX(-50%)',
                background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.12)',
                border: '1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.2)',
                borderRadius: 8,
                color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.75)',
                fontFamily: 'Montserrat, sans-serif',
                fontSize: 12,
                fontWeight: 600,
                padding: '8px 20px',
                cursor: 'pointer',
                letterSpacing: '0.08em',
                transition: 'background 0.15s ease',
              }}
              onMouseEnter={(e) =>
                (e.currentTarget.style.background = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.20)')
              }
              onMouseLeave={(e) =>
                (e.currentTarget.style.background = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.12)')
              }
            >
              ↺ REPLAY
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      </MemoryRouter>
    );
  },
};

   Story 2 — Logo em tamanhos diferentes

design-system-componentes-multitaginput · ./src/stories/components/MultiTagInput.stories.tsx
Input estilo "tag" — converte cada valor terminado por separator (default ";"), Enter ou blur em uma chip removível. Visual aprimorado: chips com ícone de envelope, cor primary suave e botão de remoção destacado.
Prop types (react-docgen) 7 prop types 
Component: src\components\ui\multi-tag-input.tsx::MultiTagInput

onChange: (next: string[]) => void

 * Caracter usado para separar os e-mails ao colar/digitar (default ";")
 */

 * Mostra o ícone de envelope dentro de cada chip (default true para email)
 */

const Interativo = () => {
  const [checked, setChecked] = useState(true);
  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col gap-6">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
        <Switch
          id="demo-switch"
          checked={checked}
          onCheckedChange={setChecked}
        />
        <Label htmlFor="demo-switch" className="text-sm cursor-pointer select-none">
          {checked ? "Ativo" : "Inativo"}
        </Label>
      </div>
      <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
        Estado: <strong>{checked ? "ligado" : "desligado"}</strong>
      </p>
    </div>
  );
};
Todas as variantes story ok 
const TodasAsVariantes = () => (
  <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
    {[
      { label: "On (ativo)", checked: true, disabled: false },
      { label: "Off (inativo)", checked: false, disabled: false },
      { label: "On — desabilitado", checked: true, disabled: true },
      { label: "Off — desabilitado", checked: false, disabled: true },
    ].map(({ label, checked, disabled }) => (
      <div key={label} className="flex items-center gap-3">
        <Switch checked={checked} disabled={disabled} />
        <span className="text-sm text-foreground">{label}</span>
      </div>
    ))}
  </div>
);
Exemplo — Status de cliente story ok 
const ExemploClienteStatus = () => {
  const [clientes, setClientes] = useState([
    { id: "1", nome: "Carlos Silva", ativo: true },
    { id: "2", nome: "Tech Corp LTDA", ativo: true },
    { id: "3", nome: "Ana Beatriz Silva", ativo: false },
  ]);

  return (
    <div className="space-y-2 w-72">
      {clientes.map((c) => (
        <div
          key={c.id}
          className="flex items-center justify-between rounded-md border border-border bg-card px-3 py-2.5"
        >
          <span className="text-sm font-medium">{c.nome}</span>
          <Switch
            checked={c.ativo}
            onCheckedChange={() =>
              setClientes((prev) =>
                prev.map((x) => (x.id === c.id ? { ...x, ativo: !x.ativo } : x))
              )
            }
          />
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
};

Interativo — Demo com tabela story ok 
const Interativo = () => {
  const PAGE_SIZE = 10;
  const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
  const totalPages = Math.ceil(FAKE_DATA.length / PAGE_SIZE);
  const rows = FAKE_DATA.slice((page - 1) * PAGE_SIZE, page * PAGE_SIZE);

  return (
    <div className="w-full max-w-3xl border border-border rounded-lg overflow-hidden bg-card">
      <table className="w-full text-sm">
        <thead className="bg-muted/40 border-b border-border">
          <tr>
            {["ID", "Solicitante", "Ativo", "Status"].map((h) => (
              <th
                key={h}
                className="text-left px-4 py-2.5 text-xs font-heading font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider"
              >
                {h}
              </th>
            ))}
          </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
          {rows.map((row, i) => (
            <tr
              key={row.id}
              className={`border-b border-border last:border-0 ${i % 2 === 0 ? "" : "bg-muted/10"}`}
            >
              <td className="px-4 py-2.5 font-mono text-xs text-primary">{row.id}</td>
              <td className="px-4 py-2.5 text-foreground">{row.solicitante}</td>
              <td className="px-4 py-2.5 font-mono text-foreground">{row.ativo}</td>
              <td className="px-4 py-2.5 text-muted-foreground">{row.status}</td>
            </tr>
          ))}
        </tbody>
      </table>

      <TablePagination
        currentPage={page}
        totalPages={totalPages}
        onPageChange={setPage}
        totalItems={FAKE_DATA.length}
        itemsPerPage={PAGE_SIZE}
        itemLabel="solicitações"
      />
    </div>
  );
};

import type { Meta, StoryObj } from '@storybook/react-vite';

const meta: Meta = {
  title: 'Design System / Tokens / Tipografia',
  parameters: { layout: 'fullscreen' },
};
export default meta;
type Story = StoryObj;

const TYPE_SCALE = [
  { token: '--primitive-font-size-xs',   name: 'xs',   rem: '0.75rem', px: '12px', weight: '400', use: 'Captions, hints, labels auxiliares' },
  { token: '--primitive-font-size-sm',   name: 'sm',   rem: '0.875rem', px: '14px', weight: '400/500', use: 'Corpo secundário, labels de campo' },
  { token: '--primitive-font-size-base', name: 'base', rem: '1rem', px: '16px', weight: '400', use: 'Corpo de texto padrão' },
  { token: '--primitive-font-size-lg',   name: 'lg',   rem: '1.125rem', px: '18px', weight: '500/600', use: 'Subtítulos, labels destacados' },
  { token: '--primitive-font-size-xl',   name: 'xl',   rem: '1.25rem', px: '20px', weight: '600', use: 'Títulos de seção' },
  { token: '--primitive-font-size-2xl',  name: '2xl',  rem: '1.5rem', px: '24px', weight: '700', use: 'Títulos de página' },
  { token: '--primitive-font-size-3xl',  name: '3xl',  rem: '1.875rem', px: '30px', weight: '700', use: 'KPIs, números grandes' },
  { token: '--primitive-font-size-4xl',  name: '4xl',  rem: '2.25rem', px: '36px', weight: '800', use: 'Títulos de destaque / hero' },
];

const SEMANTIC_TYPES = [
  { name: 'Título de Página',  classes: 'text-2xl font-bold font-heading', sample: 'Visão Geral do Sistema' },
  { name: 'Título de Seção',   classes: 'text-lg font-semibold font-heading', sample: 'Solicitações Recentes' },
  { name: 'Label de Campo',    classes: 'text-sm font-medium', sample: 'Nome do Cliente' },
  { name: 'Corpo de Texto',    classes: 'text-sm', sample: 'Texto corrido padrão para descrições e informações gerais do sistema.' },
  { name: 'Caption / Hint',   classes: 'text-xs text-muted-foreground', sample: 'Atualizado há 5 minutos' },
  { name: 'KPI / Número',      classes: 'text-3xl font-bold font-heading', sample: 'R$ 45,2M' },
  { name: 'Badge / Chip',      classes: 'text-xs font-medium', sample: 'Em Execução' },

];

export const Escala: Story = {
  name: '1 · Escala Tipográfica',
  render: () => (
    <div className="p-8 bg-background min-h-screen">
      <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold font-heading text-foreground mb-2">Escala Tipográfica</h1>
        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-8">Base 16px. Família principal: <strong>Inter</strong> (body), <strong>Montserrat</strong> (heading).</p>
        <div className="space-y-2">
          {TYPE_SCALE.map((t) => (
            <div key={t.name} className="flex items-center gap-6 py-4 border-b border-border last:border-0">
              <div className="w-16 text-right flex-shrink-0">
                <span className="text-xs font-mono text-muted-foreground">{t.name}</span>
              </div>
              <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                <span style={{ fontSize: t.rem }} className="text-foreground font-body">
                  ABCDEFGH abcdefgh 0123456789
                </span>
              </div>
              <div className="flex-shrink-0 text-right space-y-0.5">
                <p className="text-xs font-mono text-muted-foreground">{t.rem} / {t.px}</p>
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{t.use}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  ),
};

export const Semantica: Story = {
  name: '2 · Uso Semântico',
  render: () => (
    <div className="p-8 bg-background min-h-screen">
      <div className="max-w-3xl mx-auto">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold font-heading text-foreground mb-2">Tipografia Semântica</h1>
        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-8">Como cada nível tipográfico é aplicado na interface.</p>
        <div className="space-y-6">
          {SEMANTIC_TYPES.map((t) => (
            <div key={t.name} className="flex flex-col gap-1 pb-6 border-b border-border last:border-0">

import type { Meta, StoryObj } from "@storybook/react-vite";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Toaster } from "@/components/ui/sonner";
import { toast } from "sonner";

const meta: Meta = {
  title: "Design System / Componentes / Toast (Sonner)",
  parameters: {
    layout: "centered",
    docs: {
      description: {
        component:
          "Notificações temporárias (toasts) via [Sonner](https://sonner.emilkowal.ski/). Usar para feedback de ação de curta duração — sucesso, erro, info. Para mensagens persistentes inline use `Alert`. Há **uma única `<Toaster />`** montada na raiz do app (`App.tsx`); aqui ela é incluída para demonstração isolada.",
      },
    },
  },
  tags: ["autodocs"],
  decorators: [
    (Story) => (
      <>
        <Story />
        <Toaster />
      </>
    ),
  ],
};

export default meta;
type Story = StoryObj;

export const Sucesso: Story = {
  render: () => (
    <Button onClick={() => toast.success("Boleta executada com sucesso")}>
      Disparar sucesso
    </Button>
  ),
};

export const Erro: Story = {
  render: () => (
    <Button
      variant="destructive"
      onClick={() => toast.error("Falha ao avançar boleta — verifique a boleta pai")}
    >
      Disparar erro
    </Button>
  ),
};

export const Info: Story = {
  render: () => (
    <Button
      variant="outline"
      onClick={() => toast.info("Sincronização com B3 em andamento...")}
    >
      Disparar info
    </Button>
  ),
};

export const ComAcao: Story = {
  name: "Com ação (undo)",
  render: () => (
    <Button
      variant="outline"
      onClick={() =>
        toast("Boleta movida para Em Execução", {
          action: {
            label: "Desfazer",
            onClick: () => toast.message("Movimentação revertida"),
          },
        })
      }
    >
      Disparar com ação
    </Button>
  ),
};

export const Promise: Story = {
  name: "Promise (loading + resolução)",
  render: () => (
    <Button
      onClick={() =>
        toast.promise(
          new Promise<string>((resolve) =>
            setTimeout(() => resolve("Replicação concluída"), 1500),
          ),
          {
            loading: "Replicando boleta em custódia...",
            success: (msg) => msg,
            error: "Falha na replicação",
          },
        )
      }
    >
      Disparar promise
    </Button>
  ),
};

./src/stories/components/AppHeader.stories.tsx:
import type { Meta, StoryObj } from '@storybook/react-vite';
import { Search, Bell, Moon, Sun, PanelLeft } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';

const meta: Meta = {
  title: 'Design System / Componentes / AppHeader',
  tags: ['autodocs'],
  parameters: {
    layout: 'fullscreen',
    docs: {
      description: {
        component: `
## AppHeader — Barra Superior

Barra de navegação superior da aplicação Horizon.

### Anatomia
- **Esquerda**: SidebarTrigger + Breadcrumbs
- **Direita**: Busca · Notificações · Toggle Tema · Avatar

### Regra de hover para ícones
Todo botão de ícone no header usa o padrão:

\`\`\`tsx
className="text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground"
\`\`\`

Isso garante que o ícone fique **branco** sobre o fundo **navy escuro** do \`--accent\`
tanto em **light mode** quanto em **dark mode**.

| Token | Light Mode | Dark Mode |
|-------|-----------|-----------|
| \`--accent\` | \`210 50% 24%\` (navy) | \`210 50% 24%\` (navy) |
| \`--accent-foreground\` | \`0 0% 100%\` (branco) | \`38 30% 93%\` (creme) |

> **Nunca usar** \`hover:text-foreground\` em ícones sobre fundo accent — o foreground
> em light mode é navy escuro, invisível sobre fundo navy.
        `,
      },
    },
  },
};
export default meta;
type Story = StoryObj;

const HeaderPreview = ({ theme }: { theme: 'light' | 'dark' }) => (
  <header className="h-14 border-b border-border flex items-center justify-between px-4 bg-background-secondary">
    {/* Esquerda */}
    <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
      <Button
        variant="ghost"
        size="icon"
        aria-label="Alternar sidebar"
        className="text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground"
      >
        <PanelLeft className="h-4 w-4" />
      </Button>
      <nav aria-label="Breadcrumb">
        <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Dashboard</span>
      </nav>
    </div>

    {/* Direita */}
    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
      <Button
        variant="ghost"
        size="icon"
        aria-label="Buscar"
        className="text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground"
      >
        <Search className="h-4 w-4" />
      </Button>
      <Button
        variant="ghost"
        size="icon"
        aria-label="Notificações"
        className="text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground"
      >
        <Bell className="h-4 w-4" />
      </Button>
      <Button
        variant="ghost"
        size="icon"
        aria-label="Alternar tema"
        className="text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground"
      >
        {theme === 'dark' ? <Sun className="h-4 w-4" /> : <Moon className="h-4 w-4" />}
      </Button>
      <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-primary flex items-center justify-center text-primary-foreground text-xs font-heading font-bold ml-2">
        H
      </div>
    </div>
  </header>
);

export const LightMode: Story = {
  name: 'Light Mode',
  render: (_, context) => (
    <HeaderPreview theme={(context.globals.theme as 'light' | 'dark') ?? 'light'} />
  ),
};

export const DarkMode: Story = {
  name: 'Dark Mode',
  globals: { theme: 'dark' },
  render: (_, context) => (
    <HeaderPreview theme={(context.globals.theme as 'light' | 'dark') ?? 'dark'} />
  ),
};

/**
 * Demonstração do estado de hover no ícone.
 * O fundo `--accent` (navy) exige ícone branco (`--accent-foreground`).
 */
export const HoverState: Story = {
  name: 'Hover — Ícone branco sobre navy',
  render: () => (
    <div className="flex flex-col gap-6 p-8 bg-background min-h-screen">
      <h2 className="text-sm font-heading font-semibold text-foreground uppercase tracking-wider">
        Comportamento de hover — header icons
      </h2>

      {/* Estado normal */}
      <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground font-body">Estado normal</p>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 p-3 bg-background-secondary rounded-lg border w-fit">
          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon"
            className="text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground">
            <Search className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon"
            className="text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground">
            <Bell className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon"
            className="text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground">
            <Moon className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Estado hover simulado */}
      <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground font-body">Estado hover (simulado)</p>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 p-3 bg-background-secondary rounded-lg border w-fit">
          {/* Simula hover fixo com as classes inline */}
          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon"
            className="bg-accent text-accent-foreground">
            <Search className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon"
            className="bg-accent text-accent-foreground">
            <Bell className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon"
            className="bg-accent text-accent-foreground">
            <Moon className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Token reference */}
      <div className="flex flex-col gap-3">
        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground font-body uppercase tracking-wider">Tokens utilizados</p>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 max-w-sm">
          <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
            <div className="h-10 rounded-md border" style={{ background: 'hsl(210 50% 24%)' }} />
            <span className="text-xs font-mono text-muted-foreground">--accent</span>
            <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Fundo hover</span>
          </div>
          <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
            <div className="h-10 rounded-md border" style={{ background: 'hsl(0 0% 100%)', outline: '1px solid hsl(214 20% 88%)' }} />
            <span className="text-xs font-mono text-muted-foreground">--accent-foreground</span>
            <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Cor do ícone</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Regra */}
      <div className="bg-muted rounded-lg p-4 font-mono text-xs text-muted-foreground max-w-lg">
        <p className="text-foreground font-semibold mb-2">Regra de implementação</p>
        <p>className="text-muted-foreground</p>

        <p className="line-through opacity-60 pl-4">hover:text-foreground</p>
      </div>
    </div>
  ),
};

/* ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 * Utilitários de download
 *
 * • SVG  — serializa o <svg> que já está renderizado no DOM, força um
 *          viewBox/size de 24x24 e estiliza com stroke="currentColor"
 *          (que resolve para preto quando o SVG é aberto isoladamente).
 *          Fundo SEMPRE transparente (não há <rect> de background).
 *
 * • PNG  — converte o mesmo SVG em data URL, carrega numa <img>, desenha
 *          em um <canvas> de 512x512 e exporta via canvas.toBlob('image/png').
 *          Canvas tem fundo transparente por padrão (não preenchemos).
 * ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

function triggerDownload(url: string, filename: string) {
  const a = document.createElement("a");
  a.href = url;
  a.download = filename;
  document.body.appendChild(a);
  a.click();
  document.body.removeChild(a);
}

function buildExportableSvg(svgEl: SVGSVGElement, sizePx: number): string {
  const clone = svgEl.cloneNode(true) as SVGSVGElement;
  // Garante atributos essenciais para uso isolado
  clone.setAttribute("xmlns", "http://www.w3.org/2000/svg");
  clone.setAttribute("width", String(sizePx));
  clone.setAttribute("height", String(sizePx));
  // Lucide usa stroke="currentColor"; ao abrir o SVG isolado, currentColor
  // fica preto. Se quiser garantir, descomente a linha abaixo.
  // clone.setAttribute("color", "#000");
  if (!clone.getAttribute("viewBox")) {
    clone.setAttribute("viewBox", "0 0 24 24");
  }
  // Remove classes do React/Tailwind (cosmético — não afeta render isolado)
  clone.removeAttribute("class");
  return new XMLSerializer().serializeToString(clone);
}

function downloadIconAsSvg(svgEl: SVGSVGElement, name: string) {
  const svgString = buildExportableSvg(svgEl, 24);
  const xml = '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>\n' + svgString;
  const blob = new Blob([xml], { type: "image/svg+xml;charset=utf-8" });
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  triggerDownload(url, `${name}.svg`);
  // Pequeno delay para garantir que o navegador iniciou o download antes do revoke
  window.setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(url), 1000);
}

function downloadIconAsPng(svgEl: SVGSVGElement, name: string, sizePx = 512) {
  const svgString = buildExportableSvg(svgEl, sizePx);
  const svgBlob = new Blob([svgString], { type: "image/svg+xml;charset=utf-8" });
  const svgUrl = URL.createObjectURL(svgBlob);

  const img = new Image();
  img.crossOrigin = "anonymous";
  img.onload = () => {
    const canvas = document.createElement("canvas");
    canvas.width = sizePx;
    canvas.height = sizePx;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");
    if (!ctx) {
      URL.revokeObjectURL(svgUrl);
      return;
    }
    // NÃO preenchemos o canvas → fundo permanece transparente
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, sizePx, sizePx);
    ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, sizePx, sizePx);
    URL.revokeObjectURL(svgUrl);

    canvas.toBlob((blob) => {
      if (!blob) return;
      const pngUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
      triggerDownload(pngUrl, `${name}.png`);
      window.setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(pngUrl), 1000);
    }, "image/png");
  };
  img.onerror = () => URL.revokeObjectURL(svgUrl);
  img.src = svgUrl;
}

/* ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 * Card individual de ícone
 * ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

interface IconCardProps {
  name: string;
  Icon: React.ElementType;
  query: string;
  isCopied: boolean;
  onCopy: (name: string) => void;
}

function IconCard({ name, Icon, query, isCopied, onCopy }: IconCardProps) {
  const ref = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  const getSvgEl = (): SVGSVGElement | null => {
    return (ref.current?.querySelector("svg") as SVGSVGElement | null) ?? null;
  };

  const handleDownloadSvg = (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    const svg = getSvgEl();
    if (svg) downloadIconAsSvg(svg, name);
  };

  const handleDownloadPng = (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    const svg = getSvgEl();
    if (svg) downloadIconAsPng(svg, name);
  };

  return (
    <div
      ref={ref}
      className={`relative group/card rounded-lg border bg-card transition-colors ${
        isCopied
          ? "border-primary bg-primary/10"
          : "border-border hover:bg-accent/30"
      }`}
    >
      {/* Action buttons — visíveis no hover */}
      <div
        className="absolute top-1 right-1 z-10 flex gap-0.5 opacity-0 group-hover/card:opacity-100 focus-within:opacity-100 transition-opacity"
        onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
      >
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={handleDownloadSvg}
          title={`Baixar ${name}.svg (fundo transparente)`}
          aria-label={`Baixar ${name} como SVG transparente`}
          className="px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[9px] font-mono font-semibold rounded bg-background/90 backdrop-blur-sm border border-border text-muted-foreground hover:bg-primary hover:text-primary-foreground hover:border-primary transition-colors"
        >
          SVG
        </button>
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={handleDownloadPng}
          title={`Baixar ${name}.png 512px (fundo transparente)`}
          aria-label={`Baixar ${name} como PNG transparente`}
          className="px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[9px] font-mono font-semibold rounded bg-background/90 backdrop-blur-sm border border-border text-muted-foreground hover:bg-primary hover:text-primary-foreground hover:border-primary transition-colors"
        >
          PNG
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Body — clique copia o nome */}
      <button
        type="button"
        onClick={() => onCopy(name)}
        title={isCopied ? "Copiado!" : `Clique para copiar "${name}"`}
        className="w-full flex flex-col items-center gap-2 p-3 cursor-pointer text-left bg-transparent rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-ring"
      >
        <Icon
          className={`h-5 w-5 ${
            isCopied ? "text-primary" : "text-foreground"
          }`}
        />
        <span className="text-[9px] text-muted-foreground font-mono text-center leading-tight break-all">
          {isCopied ? (
            <span className="text-primary font-semibold">Copiado!</span>
          ) : (
            <HighlightedName name={name} query={query} />
          )}
        </span>
      </button>
    </div>
  );
}

/**
 * Destaca o trecho do nome que casou com a busca, sem usar `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`.
 */
function HighlightedName({ name, query }: { name: string; query: string }) {
  if (!query) return <>{name}</>;
  const idx = name.toLowerCase().indexOf(query.toLowerCase());
  if (idx === -1) return <>{name}</>;
  return (
    <>
      {name.slice(0, idx)}
      <mark className="bg-primary/30 text-primary rounded-sm px-0.5">
        {name.slice(idx, idx + query.length)}
      </mark>
      {name.slice(idx + query.length)}
    </>
  );
}

function IconGrid() {
  const [query, setQuery] = useState("");
  const [copied, setCopied] = useState<string | null>(null);

  /** Filtra grupos e seus ícones — esconde grupos sem matches. */
  const filteredGroups = useMemo(() => {
    const q = query.trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!q) return iconGroups;
    return iconGroups
      .map((g) => ({
        ...g,
        icons: g.icons.filter((i) => i.name.toLowerCase().includes(q)),
      }))
      .filter((g) => g.icons.length > 0);
  }, [query]);

  const totalIcons = useMemo(
    () => iconGroups.reduce((sum, g) => sum + g.icons.length, 0),
    [],
  );
  const matchedCount = useMemo(
    () => filteredGroups.reduce((sum, g) => sum + g.icons.length, 0),
    [filteredGroups],
  );

  const copyName = async (name: string) => {
    try {
      await navigator.clipboard.writeText(name);
      setCopied(name);
      window.setTimeout(() => setCopied((c) => (c === name ? null : c)), 1200);
    } catch {
      /* clipboard pode estar bloqueado */
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="p-2">
      {/* ─── Search bar (sticky no topo) ─────────────────────────────────── */}
      <div className="sticky top-0 z-10 -mx-2 px-2 py-3 mb-6 bg-background/95 backdrop-blur supports-[backdrop-filter]:bg-background/80 border-b border-border">
        <div className="relative">
          <Search className="pointer-events-none absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 h-4 w-4 text-muted-foreground" />
          <input
            type="search"
            value={query}
            onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="Buscar ícone por nome (ex.: chevron, user, file)…"
            aria-label="Buscar ícone"
            autoFocus
            className="w-full h-10 pl-9 pr-24 rounded-md border border-input bg-background text-sm text-foreground placeholder:text-muted-foreground focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 focus:ring-offset-background"
          />
          {query && (
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={() => setQuery("")}
              aria-label="Limpar busca"
              className="absolute right-2 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center h-6 w-6 rounded hover:bg-muted text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground"
            >
              <X className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
            </button>
          )}
        </div>

        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mt-2 px-1">
          <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground">
            {query ? (
              <>
                <span className="text-foreground font-semibold">{matchedCount}</span>{" "}
                de {totalIcons} ícones · clique para copiar nome · passe o mouse
                e clique <span className="font-mono text-foreground">SVG</span>/
                <span className="font-mono text-foreground">PNG</span> para baixar
              </>
            ) : (
              <>
                <span className="text-foreground font-semibold">{totalIcons}</span>{" "}
                ícones · clique para copiar nome · passe o mouse e clique{" "}
                <span className="font-mono text-foreground">SVG</span>/
                <span className="font-mono text-foreground">PNG</span> para baixar
                (fundo transparente)
              </>
            )}
          </p>
          {query && matchedCount === 0 && (
            <p className="text-[11px] text-warning">Nenhum ícone encontrado</p>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* ─── Grids por grupo ─────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
      {filteredGroups.length === 0 ? (
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center py-16 px-4 text-center">
          <Search className="h-10 w-10 text-muted-foreground/50 mb-3" />
          <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">
            Nenhum ícone corresponde a “{query}”
          </p>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
            Verifique a grafia (PascalCase) ou tente um termo mais curto.
          </p>
          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={() => setQuery("")}
            className="mt-4 text-xs font-medium text-primary hover:underline"
          >
            Limpar busca
          </button>
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="space-y-10">
          {filteredGroups.map((group) => (
            <div key={group.label}>
              <h3 className="text-xs font-heading font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-4">
                {group.label}{" "}
                <span className="text-muted-foreground/60 normal-case font-normal">
                  ({group.icons.length})
                </span>
              </h3>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-4 sm:grid-cols-6 md:grid-cols-8 lg:grid-cols-10 gap-2">
                {group.icons.map(({ name, icon: Icon }) => (
                  <IconCard
                    key={name}
                    name={name}
                    Icon={Icon}
                    query={query}
                    isCopied={copied === name}
                    onCopy={copyName}
                  />
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

export const TodosOsIcones: Story = {
  name: "Todos os Ícones",
  render: () => <IconGrid />,
};

export const UsageGuide: Story = {
  name: "Guia de Uso",
  render: () => (

function isLight(hex: string) {
  const r = parseInt(hex.slice(1, 3), 16);
  const g = parseInt(hex.slice(3, 5), 16);
  const b = parseInt(hex.slice(5, 7), 16);
  return (r * 299 + g * 587 + b * 114) / 1000 > 128;
}

function Swatch({ shade, hex, label }: { shade: string; hex: string; label?: string }) {
  const textColor = isLight(hex) ? '#111827' : '#F9FAFB';
  return (
    <div
      style={{ backgroundColor: hex, color: textColor }}
      className="flex flex-col justify-end p-3 rounded-lg min-h-[80px] relative"
      title={hex}
    >
      {label && (
        <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider opacity-80 mb-0.5">
          {label}
        </span>
      )}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <span className="text-sm font-semibold">{shade}</span>
        <span className="text-xs font-mono opacity-70">{hex}</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function Palette({ name, swatches }: { name: string; swatches: { shade: string; hex: string; label?: string }[] }) {
  return (
    <div className="mb-10">
      <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold uppercase tracking-widest text-muted-foreground mb-3">{name}</h3>
      <div className="grid grid-cols-11 gap-2">
        {swatches.map((s) => (
          <Swatch key={s.shade} {...s} />
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function TableTokenSwatch({
  name,
  cssVar,
  varName,
  desc,
  used,
}: {
  name: string;
  cssVar: string;
  varName: string;
  desc: string;
  used: string;
}) {
  return (
    <div className="flex items-start gap-4 p-4 rounded-xl border bg-card">
      <div
        className="w-14 h-14 rounded-lg flex-shrink-0 border border-border"
        style={{ backgroundColor: cssVar }}
      />
      <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
        <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-foreground">{name}</p>
        <p className="text-xs font-mono text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">{varName}</p>
        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">{desc}</p>
        <p className="text-[11px] text-primary mt-1">
          <span className="opacity-70">Usado em:</span> {used}
        </p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function SemanticSwatch({ name, cssVar, desc }: { name: string; cssVar: string; desc: string }) {
  return (
    <div className="flex items-start gap-4 p-4 rounded-xl border bg-card">
      <div
        className="w-14 h-14 rounded-lg flex-shrink-0 border border-black/10"
        style={{ backgroundColor: `var(${cssVar})` }}
      />
      <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
        <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-foreground">{name}</p>
        <p className="text-xs font-mono text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">{cssVar}</p>
        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">{desc}</p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

Loading

design-system-páginas-loading · ./src/stories/pages/Loading.stories.tsx
